 succeeded in 2469ms:
   1: /**
   2:  * graph_export — browser-side PNG + JSON downloads for ClaimGraph.
   3:  *
   4:  * `exportPNG(cy)` returns a Promise<Blob> via cytoscape's `cy.png({...,
   5:  * output: 'blob-promise'})`. 4x scale for retina-grade output.
   6:  *
   7:  * `exportJSON(payload)` produces a Blob whose body is the canonicalized
   8:  * elements JSON: positions stripped, nodes+edges sorted by id, keys
   9:  * recursively sorted, no whitespace. Mirrors backend
  10:  * `src/polaris_graph/api/graph_route.py:206-216` (modulo Python
  11:  * `ensure_ascii=True` vs JSON.stringify; consumer hashes the canonical
  12:  * form, so non-ASCII characters serialized differently between Python
  13:  * and JS will not byte-match. Documented; OK for v1 since labels are
  14:  * latin-1 by convention).
  15:  *
  16:  * `triggerDownload(blob, filename)` uses URL.createObjectURL + temp
  17:  * `<a download>` click, then revokes the URL after the click is
  18:  * dispatched.
  19:  */
  20: 
  21: import type cytoscape from "cytoscape";
  22: 
  23: import type { GraphPayload } from "@/lib/api";
  24: 
  25: export async function exportPNG(
  26:   cy: cytoscape.Core | null,
  27: ): Promise<Blob | null> {
  28:   if (!cy) return null;
  29:   const result = await cy.png({
  30:     full: true,
  31:     scale: 4,
  32:     output: "blob-promise",
  33:   });
  34:   return result as Blob;
  35: }
  36: 
  37: function sortKeys(value: unknown): unknown {
  38:   if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.map(sortKeys);
  39:   if (value && typeof value === "object") {
  40:     const sorted: Record<string, unknown> = {};
  41:     for (const k of Object.keys(value as Record<string, unknown>).sort()) {
  42:       sorted[k] = sortKeys((value as Record<string, unknown>)[k]);
  43:     }
  44:     return sorted;
  45:   }
  46:   return value;
  47: }
  48: 
  49: export function exportJSON(payload: GraphPayload): Blob {
  50:   const nodes = payload.elements.nodes
  51:     .map((n) => {
  52:       // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars
  53:       const { position: _drop, ...rest } = n;
  54:       return rest;
  55:     })
  56:     .sort((a, b) =>
  57:       a.data.id < b.data.id ? -1 : a.data.id > b.data.id ? 1 : 0,
  58:     );
  59:   const edges = [...payload.elements.edges].sort((a, b) =>
  60:     a.data.id < b.data.id ? -1 : a.data.id > b.data.id ? 1 : 0,
  61:   );
  62:   const canonical = JSON.stringify(sortKeys({ nodes, edges }));
  63:   return new Blob([canonical], { type: "application/json" });
  64: }
  65: 
  66: export function triggerDownload(blob: Blob, filename: string): void {
  67:   const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  68:   const a = document.createElement("a");
  69:   a.href = url;
  70:   a.download = filename;
  71:   document.body.appendChild(a);
  72:   a.click();
  73:   document.body.removeChild(a);
  74:   // Revoke after the click has been dispatched to free memory.
  75:   setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(url), 0);
  76: }

  28: // `react-cytoscapejs` is SSR-unsafe; dynamic-import as client-only.
  29: const CytoscapeComponent = dynamic(() => import("react-cytoscapejs"), {
  30:   ssr: false,
  31: });
  32: 
  33: interface HoverState {
  34:   id: string;
  35:   type: string;
  36:   label: string;
  37:   tier?: string;
  38:   source_url?: string;
  39:   x: number;
  40:   y: number;
  41: }
  42: 
  43: interface ClaimGraphProps {
  44:   payload: GraphPayload;
  45:   selectedNodeId: string | null;
  46:   searchQuery: string;
  47:   snowballHighlightIds: Set<string> | null;
  48:   setSelectedNodeId: (id: string | null) => void;
  49:   onCyReady?: (cy: cytoscape.Core | null) => void;
  50: }
  51: 
  52: export function ClaimGraph({
  53:   payload,
  54:   selectedNodeId,
  55:   searchQuery,
  56:   snowballHighlightIds,
  57:   setSelectedNodeId,
  58:   onCyReady,
  59: }: ClaimGraphProps) {
  60:   const [cyInstance, _setCyInstance] = useState<cytoscape.Core | null>(null);
  61:   const setCyInstance = (cy: cytoscape.Core | null) => {
  62:     _setCyInstance(cy);
  63:     onCyReady?.(cy);
  64:   };
  65:   const [hover, setHover] = useState<HoverState | null>(null);
  66: 
  67:   const { elements, layout } = useMemo(() => {
  68:     const hasPositions =
  69:       payload.elements.nodes.length > 0 &&
  70:       payload.elements.nodes.every((n) => n.position != null);
  71: 
  72:     const cyNodes = payload.elements.nodes.map((n) => ({
  73:       data: n.data,
  74:       position: n.position ?? undefined,
  75:       classes: n.data.classes ?? undefined,
  76:     }));
  77:     const cyEdges = payload.elements.edges.map((e) => ({ data: e.data }));
  78: 
  79:     return {
  80:       elements: [...cyNodes, ...cyEdges],
  81:       layout: hasPositions ? LAYOUT_PRESET : LAYOUT_FCOSE,
  82:     };
  83:   }, [payload]);
  84: 
  85:   // Idempotent event registration (I-snowball-004 iter-1 P1 fix).
  86:   // I-snowball-005 iter-1 P1 fix: tap is SELECT-only, no navigation
  87:   // (page-level "Open Inspector" button now owns Inspector routing).
  88:   useEffect(() => {
  89:     if (!cyInstance) return;
  90:     const onTap = (evt: cytoscape.EventObject) => {
  91:       setSelectedNodeId(evt.target.id());
  92:     };
  93:     const onMouseover = (evt: cytoscape.EventObject) => {
  94:       const node = evt.target;
  95:       const data = node.data();
  96:       const rendered = node.renderedPosition();
  97:       setHover({
  98:         id: data.id,
  99:         type: data.type,
 100:         label: data.label,
 101:         tier: data.tier,
 102:         source_url: data.source_url,
 103:         x: rendered.x,
 104:         y: rendered.y,
 105:       });
 106:     };
 107:     const onMouseout = () => setHover(null);
 108:     cyInstance.on("tap", "node", onTap);
 109:     cyInstance.on("mouseover", "node", onMouseover);
 110:     cyInstance.on("mouseout", "node", onMouseout);
 111:     return () => {
 112:       cyInstance.off("tap", "node", onTap);
 113:       cyInstance.off("mouseover", "node", onMouseover);
 114:       cyInstance.off("mouseout", "node", onMouseout);
 115:     };
 116:   }, [cyInstance, setSelectedNodeId]);
 117: 
 118:   // Snowball-neighbor highlight (I-snowball-005).
 119:   useEffect(() => {
 120:     if (!cyInstance) return;
 121:     cyInstance.nodes().removeClass("snowball-neighbor");
 122:     if (!snowballHighlightIds) return;
 123:     cyInstance
 124:       .nodes()
 125:       .filter((n) => snowballHighlightIds.has(n.id()))
 126:       .addClass("snowball-neighbor");
 127:   }, [cyInstance, snowballHighlightIds]);
 128: 
 129:   // Search-highlight (Codex iter-2 P2-1.5 + iter-3 share-predicate fix:
 130:   // use the same `nodeMatchesQuery` helper as the list filter).
 131:   useEffect(() => {
 132:     if (!cyInstance) return;
 133:     cyInstance.nodes().removeClass("search-hit");
 134:     if (!searchQuery.trim()) return;
 135:     cyInstance
 136:       .nodes()
 137:       .filter((n) =>
 138:         nodeMatchesQuery(
 139:           {
 140:             data: {
 141:               id: n.data("id") as string,
 142:               type: n.data("type") as
 143:                 | "sentence"
 144:                 | "source"
 145:                 | "section"
 146:                 | "frame",
 147:               label: n.data("label") as string,
 148:             },
 149:           },
 150:           searchQuery,
 151:         ),
 152:       )
 153:       .addClass("search-hit");
 154:   }, [cyInstance, searchQuery]);
 155: 
 156:   // Selection sync — selected node gets a halo via .selected class.
 157:   useEffect(() => {
 158:     if (!cyInstance) return;
 159:     cyInstance.nodes().removeClass("selected");
 160:     if (selectedNodeId) {
 161:       cyInstance.getElementById(selectedNodeId).addClass("selected");
 162:     }
 163:   }, [cyInstance, selectedNodeId]);
 164: 
 165:   return (
 166:     <section
 167:       aria-label="Claim graph canvas"
 168:       data-testid="claim-graph"
 169:       className="border-border relative flex w-full flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-md border"
 170:     >
 171:       <div className="relative h-[600px] w-full">
 172:         <CytoscapeComponent
 173:           elements={elements}
 174:           style={{ width: "100%", height: "100%" }}
 175:           layout={layout}
 176:           stylesheet={STYLESHEET}
 177:           cy={(cy) => setCyInstance(cy)}
 178:         />
 179:         {hover && (
 180:           <div
 181:             role="tooltip"
 182:             className="bg-popover text-popover-foreground border-border pointer-events-none absolute z-50 max-w-xs rounded-md border px-3 py-2 text-xs shadow-md"
 183:             style={{ left: hover.x + 12, top: hover.y + 12 }}
 184:           >
 185:             <div className="font-medium">{hover.label}</div>
 186:             <div className="text-muted-foreground">{hover.type}</div>
 187:             {hover.tier && (
 188:               <div className="text-muted-foreground">{hover.tier}</div>
 189:             )}
 190:             {hover.source_url && (
 191:               <div className="text-muted-foreground truncate">
 192:                 {hover.source_url}
 193:               </div>
 194:             )}
 195:           </div>
 196:         )}
 197:       </div>
 198:       <p className="text-muted-foreground border-border border-t p-2 text-xs">
 199:         {payload.elements.nodes.length} nodes · {payload.elements.edges.length}{" "}
 200:         edges · hash {payload.elements_hash.slice(0, 12)}…
 201:       </p>
 202:     </section>
 203:   );
 204: }

  49: export interface ApiError extends Error {
  50:   status: number;
  51:   body: unknown;
  52: }
  53: 
  54: async function asJsonOrThrow<T>(response: Response): Promise<T> {
  55:   const body = await response.json().catch(() => null);
  56:   if (!response.ok) {
  57:     const error = new Error(
  58:       `POLARIS backend returned ${response.status}`,
  59:     ) as ApiError;
  60:     error.status = response.status;
  61:     error.body = body;
  62:     throw error;
  63:   }
  64:   return body as T;
  65: }

 285: export function downloadBundleAsJson(bundle: EvidenceContract): void {
 286:   const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(bundle, null, 2)], {
 287:     type: "application/json",
 288:   });
 289:   const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
 290:   const link = document.createElement("a");
 291:   link.href = url;
 292:   link.download = `polaris_bundle_${bundle.run_id}.json`;
 293:   document.body.appendChild(link);
 294:   link.click();
 295:   document.body.removeChild(link);
 296:   URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
 297: }

 299: export interface StreamEvent {
 300:   event: string;
 301:   data: Record<string, unknown>;
 302: }
 303: 
 304: /**
 305:  * Subscribe to /stream/{runId}. Returns the EventSource so the caller can
 306:  * close it. Per Phase 0 stub, the backend yields 5 deterministic events.
 307:  */
 308: export function subscribeToRun(
 309:   runId: string,
 310:   onEvent: (event: StreamEvent) => void,
 311:   onError?: (error: Event) => void,
 312: ): EventSource {
 313:   const source = new EventSource(`${BACKEND_URL}/stream/${runId}`);
 314: 
 315:   const handler = (event: MessageEvent<string>) => {
 316:     try {
 317:       const parsed = JSON.parse(event.data);
 318:       onEvent({ event: event.type, data: parsed });
 319:     } catch {
 320:       onEvent({ event: event.type, data: { raw: event.data } });
 321:     }
 322:   };
 323: 
 324:   for (const eventName of [
 325:     "scope_decision",
 326:     "retrieval_progress",
 327:     "verifier_verdict",
 328:     "section_complete",
 329:     "run_complete",
 330:   ]) {
 331:     source.addEventListener(eventName, handler);
 332:   }
 333: 
 334:   if (onError) {
 335:     source.onerror = onError;
 336:   }
 337:   return source;
 338: }

 341: // Slice 001 — Clinical Scope Discovery + Ambiguity Detection
 342: // Mirrors src/polaris_graph/scope/scope_decision.py + api/intake_route.py.

 344: 
 345: export type IntakeStatus =
 346:   | "in_scope"
 347:   | "ambiguous_needs_clarification"
 348:   | "out_of_scope"
 349:   | "refused";

 352:   | "clinical_efficacy"
 353:   | "clinical_safety"
 354:   | "clinical_diagnosis"
 355:   | "clinical_prognosis"
 356:   | "out_of_scope";

 403: export interface IntakeSuccessResponse {
 404:   error: false;
 405:   decision: IntakeScopeDecision;
 406:   server_time_utc: string;
 407: }
 408: 
 409: export interface IntakeErrorBody {
 410:   error: true;
 411:   code: "too_short" | "too_long" | "invalid_input";
 412:   message: string;
 413:   raw: string;
 414: }
 415: 
 416: export class IntakeBadRequestError extends Error {
 417:   code: IntakeErrorBody["code"];
 418:   raw: string;
 419:   constructor(body: IntakeErrorBody) {
 420:     super(body.message);
 421:     this.name = "IntakeBadRequestError";
 422:     this.code = body.code;
 423:     this.raw = body.raw;
 424:   }
 425: }
 426: 
 427: export async function runIntake(
 428:   question: string,
 429: ): Promise<IntakeSuccessResponse> {
 430:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/intake`, {
 431:     method: "POST",
 432:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 433:     body: JSON.stringify({ question }),
 434:   });
 435: 
 436:   if (response.status === 400) {
 437:     const detail = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 438:     const body = (detail?.detail ?? detail) as IntakeErrorBody | null;
 439:     if (body && body.error) {
 440:       throw new IntakeBadRequestError(body);
 441:     }
 442:   }
 443: 
 444:   return asJsonOrThrow<IntakeSuccessResponse>(response);
 445: }

 449:   slice: string;
 450:   pipeline_stages: string[];
 451: }

 454:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/intake/health`);
 455:   return asJsonOrThrow<IntakeHealthResponse>(response);
 456: }

 512: }

 515:   code: RetrievalErrorBody["code"];
 516:   decision_id: string | null;
 517:   constructor(body: RetrievalErrorBody) {
 518:     super(body.message);
 519:     this.name = "RetrievalBadRequestError";
 520:     this.code = body.code;
 521:     this.decision_id = body.decision_id;
 522:   }

 525: export async function runRetrieval(
 526:   decision: IntakeScopeDecision,
 527: ): Promise<RetrievalSuccessResponse> {
 528:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/retrieval`, {
 529:     method: "POST",
 530:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 531:     body: JSON.stringify({ decision }),
 532:   });
 533: 
 534:   if (response.status === 400) {
 535:     const detail = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 536:     const body = (detail?.detail ?? detail) as RetrievalErrorBody | null;
 537:     if (body && body.error) {
 538:       throw new RetrievalBadRequestError(body);
 539:     }
 540:   }
 541: 
 542:   return asJsonOrThrow<RetrievalSuccessResponse>(response);
 543: }

 556: 
 557: /** Convenience: count sources matching a given tier. */
 558: export function countSourcesByTier(
 559:   pool: EvidencePool,
 560:   tier: RetrievalSourceTier,
 561: ): number {
 562:   return pool.sources.filter((s) => s.tier === tier).length;
 563: }
 564: 
 565: /** Convenience: dedupe + sort sources by tier (T1 first), then by domain. */
 566: export function sortSourcesByTier(
 567:   sources: RetrievalSource[],
 568: ): RetrievalSource[] {
 569:   const tier_rank: Record<RetrievalSourceTier, number> = {
 570:     T1: 0,
 571:     T2: 1,
 572:     T3: 2,
 573:   };
 574:   return [...sources].sort((a, b) => {
 575:     const t = tier_rank[a.tier] - tier_rank[b.tier];
 576:     if (t !== 0) return t;
 577:     return a.domain.localeCompare(b.domain);
 578:   });
 579: }

 797: // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 798: // Slice 004 — Audit bundle (GPG-signed .tar.gz export)
 799: // Mirrors src/polaris_graph/api/audit_bundle_route.py.
 800: // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 801: 
 802: export interface AuditBundleErrorBody {
 803:   error: true;
 804:   code:
 805:     | "fk_chain_mismatch"
 806:     | "verdict_not_success"
 807:     | "cited_span_unreachable_after_snapshot"
 808:     | "copyrighted_span_in_bundle"
 809:     | "gpg_unavailable"
 810:     | "sign_failed";
 811:   message: string;
 812:   report_id: string | null;
 813: }
 814: 
 815: export class AuditBundleError extends Error {
 816:   code: AuditBundleErrorBody["code"];
 817:   report_id: string | null;
 818:   constructor(body: AuditBundleErrorBody) {
 819:     super(body.message);
 820:     this.name = "AuditBundleError";
 821:     this.code = body.code;
 822:     this.report_id = body.report_id;
 823:   }
 824: }
 825: 
 826: /**
 827:  * Build + download a GPG-signed audit bundle for the given research chain.
 828:  *
 829:  * Returns a Blob of the audit_<id>.tar.gz on success. On HTTP 4xx/5xx
 830:  * with a structured error body, throws AuditBundleError with the .code
 831:  * field set so callers can show specific UX (e.g. "GPG signer not
 832:  * configured" vs "report verdict not success").
 833:  */
 834: export async function downloadAuditBundle(
 835:   decision: IntakeScopeDecision,
 836:   pool: EvidencePool,
 837:   report: VerifiedReport,
 838: ): Promise<Blob> {
 839:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/audit-bundle`, {
 840:     method: "POST",
 841:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 842:     body: JSON.stringify({ decision, pool, report }),
 843:   });
 844:   if (!response.ok) {
 845:     const detail = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 846:     const body = (detail?.detail ?? detail) as AuditBundleErrorBody | null;
 847:     if (body && body.error) {
 848:       throw new AuditBundleError(body);
 849:     }
 850:     throw new Error(`Audit bundle request failed: HTTP ${response.status}`);
 851:   }
 852:   return await response.blob();
 853: }
 854: 
 855: export interface BundlePreviewByContentType {
 856:   count: number;
 857:   bytes: number;
 858: }
 859: 
 860: export interface BundlePreviewResponse {
 861:   preview_bundle_id: string;
 862:   generator_model: string;
 863:   polaris_version: string;
 864:   file_count: number;
 865:   total_bytes: number;
 866:   content_type_breakdown: Record<string, BundlePreviewByContentType>;
 867: }
 868: 
 869: export async function previewAuditBundle(
 870:   decision: IntakeScopeDecision,
 871:   pool: EvidencePool,
 872:   report: VerifiedReport,
 873: ): Promise<BundlePreviewResponse> {
 874:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/audit-bundle/preview`, {
 875:     method: "POST",
 876:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 877:     body: JSON.stringify({ decision, pool, report }),
 878:   });
 879:   if (!response.ok) {
 880:     const detail = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 881:     const body = (detail?.detail ?? detail) as AuditBundleErrorBody | null;
 882:     if (body && body.error) {
 883:       throw new AuditBundleError(body);
 884:     }
 885:     throw new Error(`Bundle preview request failed: HTTP ${response.status}`);
 886:   }
 887:   return (await response.json()) as BundlePreviewResponse;
 888: }
 889: 
 890: export interface AuditBundleHealthResponse {
 891:   status: "ok";
 892:   slice: string;
 893:   pipeline_stages: string[];
 894:   signing_backend: string;
 895: }
 896: 
 897: export async function getAuditBundleHealth(): Promise<AuditBundleHealthResponse> {
 898:   const response = await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/audit-bundle/health`);
 899:   return asJsonOrThrow<AuditBundleHealthResponse>(response);
 900: }

 990: export async function getBenchmarkSummary(
 991:   benchmark_id: string,
 992: ): Promise<string> {
 993:   const response = await fetch(
 994:     `${BACKEND_URL}/api/benchmark/${encodeURIComponent(benchmark_id)}/summary`,
 995:   );
 996:   if (!response.ok) {
 997:     throw new Error(`benchmark summary fetch failed: HTTP ${response.status}`);

 succeeded in 2067ms:
 171: 
 172:     # 6. Sentence nodes + section_member + cites edges
 173:     edges: list[ClaimEdge] = []
 174:     for section in ir.verified_report.sections:
 175:         sec_id = f"section:{_slug(section.title)}"
 176:         for sent in section.sentences:
 177:             if not sent.is_verified:
 178:                 continue
 179:             sent_id = f"sent:{sent.claim_id}"
 180:             nodes.append(ClaimNode(data=NodeData(
 181:                 id=sent_id, type="sentence",
 182:                 label=sent.text[:100], sentence_text=sent.text,
 183:             )))
 184:             edges.append(ClaimEdge(data=EdgeData(
 185:                 id=f"membersec:{sent.claim_id}:{_slug(section.title)}",
 186:                 source=sent_id, target=sec_id, edge_type="section_member",
 187:             )))
 188:             for ord_, tok in enumerate(sent.tokens):
 189:                 if tok.evidence_id not in valid_source_ids:
 190:                     continue  # defensive — should not happen given fallback creation
 191:                 edges.append(ClaimEdge(data=EdgeData(
 192:                     id=f"cite:{sent.claim_id}:{ord_}:{tok.evidence_id}",
 193:                     source=sent_id, target=f"src:{tok.evidence_id}", edge_type="cites",
 194:                 )))
 195: 
 196:     # 7. Contradicts edges (pairwise within each cluster; skip self-contradictions)
 197:     for cluster in ir.contradictions:
 198:         evidence_ids = sorted({c.evidence_id for c in cluster.claims if c.evidence_id in valid_source_ids})
 199:         for i, a in enumerate(evidence_ids):
 200:             for b in evidence_ids[i + 1:]:
 201:                 edges.append(ClaimEdge(data=EdgeData(
 202:                     id=f"contra:{cluster.cluster_id}:{a}:{b}",
 203:                     source=f"src:{a}", target=f"src:{b}", edge_type="contradicts",
 204:                 )))
 205: 
 206:     # 8. Canonical content hash (position-stripped, sorted by id)
 207:     elements_dict = GraphElements(nodes=nodes, edges=edges).model_dump(mode="json")
 208:     elements_dict["nodes"].sort(key=lambda n: n["data"]["id"])
 209:     elements_dict["edges"].sort(key=lambda e: e["data"]["id"])
 210:     for n in elements_dict["nodes"]:
 211:         n.pop("position", None)
 212:     canonical = json.dumps(elements_dict, sort_keys=True, separators=(",", ":"))
 213:     elements_hash = hashlib.sha256(canonical.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
 214: 
 215:     return GraphPayload(
 216:         elements=GraphElements(nodes=nodes, edges=edges),
 217:         run_id=ir.run_id,
 218:         elements_hash=elements_hash,
 219:         diagnostics=GraphDiagnostics(
 220:             bibliography_count=len(bib_ids),
 221:             fallback_source_count=len(missing_unique),
 222:             missing_reference_occurrence_count=sum(
 223:                 1 for eid in referenced_occurrences if eid not in bib_ids
 224:             ),
 225:             referenced_unknown_evidence_ids=missing_unique,
 226:         ),

  76: 
  77: 
  78: class ClaimEdge(BaseModel):
  79:     data: EdgeData
  80: 
  81: 
  82: class GraphElements(BaseModel):
  83:     nodes: list[ClaimNode]
  84:     edges: list[ClaimEdge]
  85: 
  86: 
  87: class GraphDiagnostics(BaseModel):
  88:     bibliography_count: int
  89:     fallback_source_count: int  # unique evidence_ids referenced but absent from bibliography
  90:     missing_reference_occurrence_count: int  # total references (with duplicates)
  91:     referenced_unknown_evidence_ids: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
  92: 
  93: 
  94: class GraphPayload(BaseModel):
  95:     elements: GraphElements
  96:     run_id: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=200)
  97:     elements_hash: str = Field(min_length=64, max_length=64)
  98:     diagnostics: GraphDiagnostics
  99:     schema_version: Literal["1.0"] = "1.0"
 100: 
 101: 
 102: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 103: # Helpers
 104: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 105: 
 106: def _slug(text: str) -> str:
 107:     return re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9]+", "_", text.lower()).strip("_")[:80] or "section"
 108: 
 109: 
 110: def _normalize_frame_status(raw: str) -> FrameStatus | None:
 111:     if raw == "pass":
 112:         return "pass"
 113:     if raw == "partial":
 114:         return "partial"
 115:     if raw.startswith("fail"):
 116:         return "fail"
 117:     return None
 118: 
 119: 
 120: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 121: # Builder (pure function — easy to test)
 122: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 123: 
 124: def build_graph_payload(ir: "AuditIR") -> GraphPayload:
 125:     """Transform AuditIR into cytoscape-format GraphPayload (deterministic)."""
 126:     # 1. Bibliography source nodes
 127:     bib_ids: set[str] = set()
 128:     nodes: list[ClaimNode] = []
 129:     for entry in ir.bibliography:
 130:         bib_ids.add(entry.evidence_id)
 131:         tier = entry.tier if entry.tier in _VALID_TIERS else None
 132:         label = (entry.statement or entry.evidence_id)[:200]
 133:         nodes.append(ClaimNode(data=NodeData(
 134:             id=f"src:{entry.evidence_id}", type="source", label=label,
 135:             tier=tier, source_url=entry.url or None,
 136:         )))
 137: 
 138:     # 2. Collect all referenced evidence_ids from sentence tokens + contradictions
 139:     referenced_occurrences: list[str] = []
 140:     for section in ir.verified_report.sections:
 141:         for sent in section.sentences:
 142:             if sent.is_verified:
 143:                 for tok in sent.tokens:
 144:                     referenced_occurrences.append(tok.evidence_id)
 145:     for cluster in ir.contradictions:
 146:         for claim in cluster.claims:
 147:             referenced_occurrences.append(claim.evidence_id)
 148:     referenced_unique = set(referenced_occurrences)
 149: 
 150:     # 3. Fallback source nodes for referenced-but-missing-from-bibliography
 151:     missing_unique = sorted(referenced_unique - bib_ids)
 152:     for eid in missing_unique:
 153:         nodes.append(ClaimNode(data=NodeData(
 154:             id=f"src:{eid}", type="source", label=eid, classes="bibliography_missing",
 155:         )))
 156:     valid_source_ids = bib_ids | set(missing_unique)
 157: 
 158:     # 4. Section nodes
 159:     for section in ir.verified_report.sections:
 160:         nodes.append(ClaimNode(data=NodeData(
 161:             id=f"section:{_slug(section.title)}", type="section",
 162:             label=section.title, section_title=section.title,
 163:         )))
 164: 
 165:     # 5. Frame nodes (FrameCoverageReport.entries per AuditIR schema)
 166:     for entry in ir.frame_coverage.entries:
 167:         nodes.append(ClaimNode(data=NodeData(
 168:             id=f"frame:{entry.entity_id}", type="frame", label=entry.entity_id,
 169:             frame_status=_normalize_frame_status(entry.status),
 170:         )))

   1: import React from 'react';
   2: import { types } from './types';
   3: import { defaults } from './defaults';
   4: import Cytoscape from 'cytoscape';
   5: import { patch } from './patch';
   6: 
   7: /**
   8:  * The `CytoscapeComponent` is a React component that allows for the declarative creation
   9:  * and modification of a Cytoscape instance, a graph visualisation.
  10:  */
  11: export default class CytoscapeComponent extends React.Component {
  12:   static get propTypes() {
  13:     return types;
  14:   }
  15: 
  16:   static get defaultProps() {
  17:     return defaults;
  18:   }
  19: 
  20:   static normalizeElements(elements) {
  21:     const isArray = elements.length != null;
  22: 
  23:     if (isArray) {
  24:       return elements;
  25:     } else {
  26:       let { nodes, edges } = elements;
  27: 
  28:       if (nodes == null) {
  29:         nodes = [];
  30:       }
  31: 
  32:       if (edges == null) {
  33:         edges = [];
  34:       }
  35: 
  36:       return nodes.concat(edges);
  37:     }
  38:   }
  39: 
  40:   constructor(props) {
  41:     super(props);
  42:     this.displayName = 'CytoscapeComponent';
  43:     this.containerRef = React.createRef();
  44:   }
  45: 
  46:   componentDidMount() {
  47:     const container = this.containerRef.current;
  48: 
  49:     const {
  50:       global,
  51:       headless,
  52:       styleEnabled,
  53:       hideEdgesOnViewport,
  54:       textureOnViewport,
  55:       motionBlur,
  56:       motionBlurOpacity,
  57:       wheelSensitivity,
  58:       pixelRatio,
  59:     } = this.props;
  60: 
  61:     const cy = (this._cy = new Cytoscape({
  62:       container,
  63:       headless,
  64:       styleEnabled,
  65:       hideEdgesOnViewport,
  66:       textureOnViewport,
  67:       motionBlur,
  68:       motionBlurOpacity,
  69:       wheelSensitivity,
  70:       pixelRatio,
  71:     }));
  72: 
  73:     if (global) {
  74:       window[global] = cy;
  75:     }
  76: 
  77:     this.updateCytoscape(null, this.props);
  78:   }
  79: 
  80:   updateCytoscape(prevProps, newProps) {
  81:     const cy = this._cy;
  82:     const { diff, toJson, get, forEach } = newProps;
  83: 
  84:     patch(cy, prevProps, newProps, diff, toJson, get, forEach);
  85: 
  86:     if (newProps.cy != null) {
  87:       newProps.cy(cy);
  88:     }
  89:   }
  90: 
  91:   componentDidUpdate(prevProps) {
  92:     this.updateCytoscape(prevProps, this.props);
  93:   }
  94: 
  95:   componentWillUnmount() {
